ACTIVE BUGS -- fix before anything else

[x] Monthly Summary lift count always 0 -- Root cause confirmed: workoutScore gate (dayScore.activityDetail.workoutScore > 0) was 0 on HealthKit-synced strength days because dayScore is frozen at write time and HealthKit sync doesn't trigger the scoring path. Exercise data and IDs were correct. Fix: removed workoutScore gate from counting block; now gates on checkedExercises.length > 0 OR cardioDone instead. utils/monthlySummary.ts. FIXED 2026-06-08.

[ ] TUTORIAL POLISH PASS -- dedicated session required. Confirmed good: spotlight animation quality, highlighting, interactive flows, app stability. Issues to fix as a batch:
  [ ] Spotlight transition lag -- NEEDS TESTFLIGHT VERIFICATION. Fix shipped 2026-05-26: for non-navigation steps, spotlight animation now starts simultaneously with bubble fade-out instead of after it, eliminating ~150ms dead time. Navigation steps unchanged (sequential required). TutorialOverlay.tsx. Cannot verify smoothness in dev build -- confirm on next TestFlight.
  [x] Auto-scroll to off-screen targets -- FIXED 2026-05-26. Added scrollToTop?: boolean to TutorialStep interface. manage_log TODAY'S TOTAL step gets scrollToTop:true -- doStepTransition detects flag, fires scrollTo({y:0, animated:false}) on all registered scroll views, waits 350ms (overlapping with bubble fade) before measuring. measureInWindow now returns valid coords since element is back in viewport. data/tutorials.ts + TutorialOverlay.tsx.
  - Demo entries mixing with real data: CONFIRMED NON-ISSUE. Spotlight lands on the demo entry row specifically, not the whole meal section. Mixed real + demo entries in same section is fine since the highlight makes it clear what the tutorial is pointing at. Removed.
  [x] End navigation -- FIXED 2026-05-26. All tutorials now return to launch point on DONE or SKIP. From tutorials list page: returns to /tutorials. From tab ? icon (ToolkitSheet): cleanup action pops the sub-screen back to the originating tab, no extra navigation. Each sub-screen cleanup action (closeExerciseLibraryTutorial, closeRecipeTutorial, closeCreatorAfterTutorial, clearTutorialScanState, deleteTutorialRecipe) does router.back() first; TutorialContext then router.push(returnRoute) for tutorials.tsx launches only. context/TutorialContext.tsx, app/tutorials.tsx, components/ToolkitSheet.tsx, app/add-food.tsx, app/recipe-builder.tsx, app/workout-library.tsx.
  [x] Tutorials list duplicate sleep variants -- FIXED 2026-05-26. Tutorials page was showing sleep_card_manual and meta_mindful alongside their primary variants (same name, confusing). Root cause: page filtered all TUTORIALS by tab instead of using TAB_TUTORIALS as source of truth. Fix: tutorials.tsx now builds list from TAB_TUTORIALS -- auto-selected variants never appear. Also future unbuilt tutorial IDs in TAB_TUTORIALS are silently skipped (getTutorialById returns undefined, filtered out). app/tutorials.tsx.
  - Launch tab: tutorials list (app/tutorials.tsx) must navigate to correct tab before starting tutorial so context is right and user lands correctly when done.
  - Stats and profile tutorials not yet interactive or polished -- dedicated pass after above issues resolved.
  [x] Meta tutorial fires on sign-in screen: auto-fires 1500ms after index.tsx mounts, but tab screens mount in background while auth/splash is the active route on fresh install. Fix: gate the timer on screen focus. app/(tabs)/index.tsx. FIXED 2026-05-26.
[x] You vs Yesterday -- burn accuracy setting not applied to net calorie calculation. Root cause: loadCals read yesterday data before settings loaded, so burnAccuracyPct was still default 100. Fix: read pj_settings into local variable at top of loadCals, use localAccuracyPct for ydBurned and ydActiveCalories. app/(tabs)/index.tsx. FIXED 2026-05-25.
[x] restoreIfFresh data loss -- AsyncStorage.multiSet overwrites ALL local keys including in-progress day data. If today's entries haven't synced to Firestore yet and a fresh install triggers restore, today's data is wiped. Fix: read existingKeys before multiSet, filter to newPairs (keys not already local) only. Local always wins on conflict. services/syncService.ts. FIXED 2026-05-25.
[x] Food log past days -- active calories shown are today's live value, not historical. Root cause 1: adjustedTarget and burned display text both used live activeCalories from useHealthKit() without isToday gate -- past days always got today's HealthKit feed. Root cause 2: log.tsx read data.caloriesBurned (cardio log calories) while day-detail read data.activeCalories (HealthKit energy) -- two different storage keys, different numbers. Fix: gate live activeCalories on isToday in both adjustedTarget calc and display text; both storage reads now use data.activeCalories || data.caloriesBurned to match day-detail and YvY. All screens now consistent. app/(tabs)/log.tsx. FIXED 2026-05-25.
[x] Food log past days -- navigating from today directly to yesterday didn't update data. Root cause: useFocusEffect set skipDateEffect.current = true then called setActiveDate(today). If activeDate was already today, no state change occurred, useEffect([activeDate]) never fired, skip flag was never consumed. First real navigation (today→yesterday) triggered useEffect, saw skip=true, cleared it, and skipped the load. Fix: added skipDateEffect.current = false at end of reload() so flag always clears after useFocusEffect's own load completes. app/(tabs)/log.tsx. FIXED 2026-05-25.
[x] Day detail workouts / home training card -- legacy focus: 'Cardio' field (stamped by Apple Health import) was leaking into home card and day detail. Home card: removed focus fallback from tag-empty path -- now shows customLabel or UNASSIGNED, consistent with workout tab. Day detail: added workoutTags state (loads from pj_settings), workout card now shows actual colored tag pills with flexWrap for multiple tags, falls back to UNASSIGNED pill. Workout header label changed to 'Workout · N/N' (removed focus/type). index.tsx + day-detail.tsx. FIXED 2026-05-25.
[x] Sign in page -- full redesign. FIXED 2026-05-25. "Already have an account? Sign In" removed -- redundant since Apple/Google ARE the sign-in buttons. welcome.tsx deleted entirely. Sign-in is now a single two-stage screen: Stage 1 shows logo + wordmark with staggered entrance animation (50ms settle delay, logo fades 900ms, wordmark fades+slides 500ms, buttons fade+slides 500ms). Apple and Google buttons height/font matched (Google font 17px, icon size 22). On sign-in success: auth buttons fade out 500ms, GET STARTED fades in 500ms -- new users only. Returning users (onboarding done) skip straight to tabs. _layout.tsx hasInitialRouted ref prevents re-navigation black flash when user signs in while already on this screen. App relaunch mid-onboarding jumps straight to Stage 2 with no animation. _layout.tsx routes !onboardingComplete to /sign-in (was /onboarding/welcome). sign-in.tsx, _layout.tsx.

[x] Food log past date nav bug -- after adding food on a past date, back navigation from add-food bounced app to today. Root cause: useFocusEffect always reset activeDate to today on every focus event regardless of whether returning from child screen. Fix: returningFromChild ref set to true before all three router.push calls (Library→add-food, meal +→add-food, entry tap→food-detail); useFocusEffect checks ref first -- if true, clears flag and reloads current date without resetting to today; activeDateRef keeps ref in sync with activeDate state. Tab switch and app background still snap to today as expected. app/(tabs)/log.tsx. FIXED 2026-05-26.
[x] FatSecret search path missing food.get -- normalizeFsSearchResult parses 4 fields from description string only, never calls food.get. Extended nutrition (fiber, sodium, cholesterol, saturated fat, sugar) was always 0 for text-searched diary entries. Root cause: saveEntry in food-detail.tsx stored food.foodNutrients (4-item array from search) directly. Fix: augment foodNutrients array in saveEntry using effectiveServing extended fields before creating diary entry -- only adds each field if not already present, so barcode path (which already has all fields) is unaffected. Note: fix is forward-only -- diary entries logged before this fix retain stale nutrient data. Re-saving any old entry via food-detail will patch it. New users unaffected. food-detail.tsx. FIXED 2026-05-26.
[x] Cardio decimal input limit -- edit cardio workout fields only allowed 1 decimal place (3.1 max). Root cause: filterDecimal in workout.tsx had .slice(0, 1) on the post-decimal portion. Fix: changed to .slice(0, 2) to allow 2 decimal places (3.11, 5.22). workout.tsx. FIXED 2026-05-26.
[x] Recents 100g bug -- stale diary entries logged before fsId was stored defaulted to 100g (no serving data to fetch). Two-layer fix: Layer 1 in openFoodDetail (add-food.tsx) -- when fsId is null on a non-custom food, resolve it in order: favorites in-memory -> myFoods in-memory -> FatSecret name search. Resolved fsId passed into foodJson so food-detail receives it. Layer 2 in food-detail.tsx -- extended on-demand useEffect safety net: if still no fsId and not custom, calls new fetchFatSecretByName() which searches by name, takes top result food_id, fetches servings. Covers any path to food-detail not via openFoodDetail. FIXED 2026-05-25.

Active calorie accuracy:
- Calorie discrepancy bug -- root cause was calorie TARGET mismatch between home (using live recommended) and log (using stale saved value). Fixed via useRecommendedCal toggle in profile -- toggle ON keeps calTarget live and in sync, toggle OFF lets user set custom static value. FIXED.
- [x] Sleep duration display clarified -- duration IS correct (sums Core+Deep+REM only, excludes Awake segments). Root issue was no communication that awake periods are excluded. FIXED. useHealthKit.ts now tracks sleepAwakeMs (value 2 samples). Sleep card shows "Xm awake during night" under bed→wake time when HealthKit data present and awake time > 0.
- Active calorie overestimate disclaimer -- small disclaimer on any screen showing active or net calories. Apple Watch and most wearables overestimate active burn. "Active calorie estimates from Apple Health may vary. Use as a guide, not a guarantee." Exact wording TBD.
- [x] Burn accuracy adjustment setting -- SHIPPED. Settings > Health section (renamed from Health Data). 4 pills: 100/90/80/70%. Raw HealthKit value always stored in pj_YYYY-MM-DD -- modifier applied at calculation time only. Existing users unaffected (default 100%). calories_today tooltip Active definition updated to mention Settings → Health. Running BMR definition added to calories_today tooltip.
- [x] Active cal goal trigger timing bug -- pre-existing bug fixed. prevActiveCalRef.current was being updated even when loaded=false, causing the crossing check to fail when HealthKit delivered data before AsyncStorage loaded. TESTFLIGHT AUDIT -- 2026-05-22
Live release build testing. Log all bugs here in real-time. Status: open / fixed.

[x] Log tab crash (CRITICAL) -- editing a past-date food entry passed date: todayKey instead of activeDate to food-detail. Saved entry to wrong date key, created sparse null entries in today's storage, crashed render on entry.name access. Fixed: date bug corrected in log.tsx, null filter + auto-cleanup on load in both log.tsx (initial useEffect + useFocusEffect) and index.tsx. FIXED 2026-05-22.
[x] Home 0/calTarget display bug -- same null entries in today's storage caused entries.reduce to throw before calTarget loaded from profile. calTarget stayed 0, adjustedTarget = 0 + activeCalories only. Fixed by null filter + storage cleanup in index.tsx loadCals (home tab loads first, cleans storage before any other screen reads it). FIXED 2026-05-22.
[x] Day detail crash -- same root cause as log tab crash. Fixed as side effect of index.tsx storage cleanup -- home tab sanitizes data on focus, day-detail reads clean storage. FIXED 2026-05-22.
[x] Add food button passing todayKey instead of activeDate -- same date bug as the edit path. Tapping + on a past-date log view navigated to add-food with date: todayKey, saving new entries to today instead of the viewed date. Fixed: date: activeDate in log.tsx line 693. FIXED 2026-05-22.
[x] Onboarding height not saving to profile -- root cause: profile-setup.tsx saved height as single `height` (total inches) but profile.tsx reads `heightFt` + `heightIn` separately. Fixed: handleContinue now saves all three (height, heightFt, heightIn). profile-setup.tsx.
[x] Home ScrollView dead zone -- could not reproduce on release build 2026-05-22. Likely resolved as side effect of layout/padding change. Closing.
[x] Log tab date does not reset on tab return -- useFocusEffect now computes today's key inline, sets skipDateEffect ref, resets activeDate, and loads today's data directly (not from stale closure). Separate useEffect([activeDate]) with mounted+skip refs handles manual date navigation without double-loading. log.tsx.
[x] Bible auto-scroll pause on touch -- onScrollBeginDrag cancels Reanimated animation so scroll view is completely free during drag; onScrollEndDrag syncs position from event and restarts withTiming from wherever user landed. bible.tsx. FIXED 2026-05-22.
[x] Bible auto-scroll choppiness -- replaced JS-thread requestAnimationFrame loop with Reanimated withTiming (linear) + useAnimatedReaction scrollTo worklet. Animation now runs entirely on UI thread, zero bridge calls per frame, immune to JS thread pressure. bible.tsx. FIXED 2026-05-22.

  [x] BUG: Sleep score inconsistency -- FIXED 2026-05-29. Root cause: five separate copies of calcSleepScore across index.tsx, day-detail.tsx, stats.tsx, head-to-head.tsx, and utils/statsData.ts had diverged. Two formula bugs present in stats.tsx, head-to-head.tsx, and statsData.ts: (1) linear durationPts (hours/goal)*40 instead of the correct cubic Math.pow(hours/goal,3)*40, (2) FEEL_BONUS map {1:0,2:10,3:20,4:30,5:40} only covered the 1-5 range -- ratings 6-10 returned 0, causing head-to-head to score a rating-8 night as 60 instead of 83. Third issue: sleepConsistencyPts (0-10 bedtime consistency bonus) was computed in index.tsx but never stored to pj_YYYY-MM-DD, so day-detail, YvY, and the stats graph always computed with 0 pts regardless of actual consistency.
    Fixes shipped: (1) All five calcSleepScore/calcSleepScoreForTrend functions updated to cubic duration + ((rating-1)/9)*30 feel formula. (2) index.tsx now writes sleepConsistencyPts to pj_YYYY-MM-DD after computing it (both on loadData and on manual sleep save). (3) day-detail.tsx reads data.sleepConsistencyPts??0 and passes it + isManual correctly. (4) YvY in index.tsx reads yd2.sleepConsistencyPts??0 and passes it. (5) statsData.ts reads data.sleepConsistencyPts??0 and passes it. (6) day-detail.tsx feel label fixed from 5-entry array (blank for ratings 6-10) to full 1-10 descriptor map. Historical data before this fix shows score without consistency pts -- going forward all views agree. Files: index.tsx, day-detail.tsx, head-to-head.tsx, stats.tsx, utils/statsData.ts.
  [x] BUG: Graph data accuracy sweep (net cal) -- FIXED 2026-05-29. Sleep score graph fixed earlier same day (statsData.ts had same FEEL_BONUS + linear bugs). Net cal root cause confirmed: statsData.ts fetchTrendData computed net as `consumed - rawActive` (no burn accuracy, no BMR) while day detail uses `consumed - round(active x accuracy/100) - BMR`. At a Glance avg (stats.tsx loadPeriodData) had a third formula: `consumed - rawActive - bmr` (BMR but no accuracy). Three different net formulas across graph / At a Glance / day detail.
    Fix: centralized net cal into two shared helpers in utils/statsData.ts so the graph, At a Glance, and day detail can never drift again:
      - buildDailyBmrMap(dateKeys): per-day BMR mirroring day detail exactly -- each day uses its own logged weight, else most recent weigh-in within prior 30 days, else 0 (no BMR). Reads pj_profile internally. Uses the date-safe birthday split parser (day-detail.tsx birthday parser also switched to split parser to match -- fixed a latent iOS UTC-midnight off-by-one there).
      - computeDayNet(consumed, dayData, dayBmr, burnAccuracyPct, isToday, minutesNow): the one true formula. net = consumed - round(active x accuracy/100) - BMR. Running (time-proportional) BMR for today, full BMR for past days. active = activeCalories || caloriesBurned.
    Wired: fetchTrendData net cal line (graph + pinned home card -- no signature change, all callers auto-correct); loadPeriodData At a Glance net (both call sites now pass burnAccuracy instead of bmr). Confirmed during audit: streaks (stats.tsx loadStreaks) already apply burn accuracy correctly. Files: utils/statsData.ts, app/(tabs)/stats.tsx, app/day-detail.tsx.
    Note: historical days with no recent weigh-in now correctly subtract 0 BMR (matching day detail) instead of a wrong number -- net values shifted from pre-fix display, but are now correct and consistent across all three views.
  [x] NetCalBarChart -- zero baseline SHIPPED 2026-05-29. New components in StatsGraphCard.tsx. The fix above exposed that net cal is correctly mostly negative (deficits), which the old GenericBarChart could not render (squashed deficits to slivers, one surplus day towering). Built per the locked spec:
      - NetCalBarChart: dynamic zero baseline (range = min(0,data)..max(0,data) so 0 is always on-chart and floats to its true position). Deficit bars hang below zero, surplus bars rise above. Auto-scales to fill height regardless of distribution. Semantic color via shared netSignColor helper: deficit = accentGreen, surplus <=300 = amber #d4860a, surplus >300 = accentRed. Emphasized zero gridline. Callout anchors on the opposite side of zero from the tapped bar so it never covers it. Full-height transparent hit target per day column so tiny near-zero bars are easy to tap.

      - Color picker removed for net cal in all three places (create flow + edit-graph flow in stats.tsx, plus StatsCardEditModal.tsx) since color is now semantic on both bar and line -- matches workoutFreq convention.   [x] Sleep score consistency points -- FIXED 2026-05-29.   [x] Sleep streaks ignored manual entries -- FIXED 2026-05-29. The sleep duration + sleep quality streak checks read data.sleepHours only, but manual sleep saves store sleepOverride (not sleepHours). So a manual night looked like zero sleep data to the streak walker and broke the chain right there, hiding all prior auto-sync days behind it. Reported live: duration streak showed 1 (should have been 4+), quality showed 1, both broken by one manual night. NOW -- Calorie Card Denominator Overhaul (Session 62, 2026-05-30)
  [x] New on-pace target denominator SHIPPED on home + log calorie cards. The old denominator was calTarget + active, where calTarget = TDEE minus pace deficit. That double counts activity: TDEE already estimates daily activity via the lifestyle multiplier, then measured active calories were added on top of it. New denominator: onPaceTarget = max(calTarget, profileBmr + adjustedActive + paceDeficit). It is BMR plus your actually measured active burn minus your pace deficit (no TDEE double count), floored at calTarget so a dead or charging watch, a non tracker, or early morning before you have moved never produces a too low target. It rises above the floor only once real active burn exceeds the activity the TDEE multiplier already assumed, and that crossover is smooth (max of two lines, no jump). paceDeficit is the signed GOAL_DEFICITS value (negative for a loss goal). Mindful is unchanged: still uses static calTarget and hides the stat row. Files: app/(tabs)/index.tsx (GOAL_DEFICITS hoisted to one module constant, onPaceTarget computed at L917, repointed calPct + calDelta + REMAINING + denominator display), app/(tabs)/log.tsx (added profileBmr + paceDeficit state set in BOTH load blocks from the active date weight, displayTarget = mindful ? calTarget : onPaceTarget drives denominator + bar + delta + remaining text). Confirmed live by Justin: on a normal day the denominator drops by roughly the active calorie amount versus the old card, which is the intended double count fix; REMAINING = onPaceTarget minus consumed.
  [x] Home card stat relabel: RUNNING NET renamed to LIVE NET (label only, value unchanged = consumed minus adjusted active minus running BMR). Long design decision: VS PACE was rejected because it equals negative REMAINING (pure redundancy), and REMAINING already encodes the pace deficit so a separate static PACE stat reads as a false thumbs up. LIVE NET is kept as the deficit lens; REMAINING is the food planning lens. Live card color stays the existing proximity logic repointed at the new target; the pace verdict (On Pace, X over) is reserved for the completed day Day Summary, never the live card, consistent with the goal hit Site 2 green at lunch decision.
  [x] Log card visual redesign SHIPPED 2026-05-30 (Justin confirmed on device): bigger macro bars in MacroStackedBar (bar height 5 to 6 to match the calorie bar, value text 13 to 15, P/C/F letter 9 to 11), P/C/F letters and the g unit colored to their macro colors (were textMuted gray), macro block pushed right (paddingLeft 22, width 140) so the bars separate from the calorie bar and group with their numbers, and the bottom row moved to a FULL WIDTH strip below the calorie+macro top row with a top border like home: REMAINING, ACTIVE, LIVE NET (3 stats, matches home 1:1), hidden in Mindful. Root reason for the full width strip: putting the stats in the left column made it taller and pushed the macro bars visually low (Justin flagged the vertical centering against the big number). File: app/(tabs)/log.tsx.
  [x] Denominator unify SHIPPED 2026-05-30 (Justin confirmed: home and log both read 1642, all three strip values match). Root cause was the manual/recommended toggle handling differing between screens: home ALWAYS recomputed and overrode the stored target (so it ignored a manual target, a latent bug) while log used the stored target and only computed BMR when no stored target existed (so log's profileBmr was 0, breaking its LIVE NET). Fix: new utils/calorieTarget.ts (loadCalorieTargets, computeBmr, resolveWeightForDate, GOAL_DEFICITS canonical) mirrors settings.tsx LIFESTYLE/TRAINING values + the robust ISO/US birthday parser. Wired into index.tsx (replaced the inline BMR/calTarget block) and log.tsx (BOTH load blocks). It honors useRecommendedCal: recommended recomputes TDEE minus deficit live, manual uses the typed target; BMR is ALWAYS computed for LIVE NET. Same weight resolution on both (that date's weigh in, else most recent within 30 days). BONUS FIX: manual calorie targets are now respected on home (previously overridden). Byte identical across home + log, cannot drift, same pattern as computeDayNet and calcSleepScore.
  [x] REQUIRED same session DONE 2026-05-30: calories_today tooltip (tooltipRegistry.ts) + cal_card tutorial (data/tutorials.ts) rewrite. calories_today: added On-Pace Target definition (BMR + today's active burn minus pace deficit, floored at daily target), reworded Remaining to on-pace target minus eaten, renamed Net to Live Net, fixed the Running BMR double dash, relabeled example to Live Net, reworded Color Coding to direction-neutral (green near target, amber drifting, red well off in EITHER direction -- the old copy implied over-only which is now wrong since color is |consumed - onPaceTarget|). cal_card tutorial: step 4 RUNNING NET to LIVE NET + bodies, CALORIES TODAY + REMAINING now reference the on-pace target. ACTIVE + COLOR CODING thresholds verified still accurate (Discipline +/-50/149, Balanced +/-150/300, Mindful none); their 2 leftover double dashes left for the tutorial copy audit item. NEW todays_total tooltip added to the log Today's Total card (i): On-Pace Target, Protein/Carbs/Fat mini-bars, Remaining, Active, Live Net, Color Coding. App-wide net label reconciliation DONE: net stat was 4 different names; now Live Net (home today-card only, it is genuinely live) and Net Cals everywhere a finalized/compared/averaged value lives (YvY card + tutorial, day-detail, head-to-head, YvY tooltip, matches stats At a Glance). All double dashes cleaned in touched copy. Interactive walkthrough for the log card deferred to SOON (toolkit shipped, walkthrough scoped separately).
  [x] GOAL HIT CONSISTENCY DONE 2026-05-30: achievements.tsx nutritionGoalDays (the missed 7th goal-hit site) now routes through evaluateCalorieGoalHit + paceTargetFromWeightGoal + buildDailyBmrMap, byte-for-byte matching achievementData.ts checkNutritionAchievements (Way 1/Way 2, burn-accuracy applied, per-day BMR, isToday false, today excluded by the pj_${today} filter). Killed both old bugs: raw activeCalories (no accuracy modifier) and the calTarget+active double-count band. weightGoal pulled from pj_profile, burnAccuracyPct + calTarget from pj_settings (profile.calTarget fallback). Pure display recompute, no pj_ records touched (count may shift up/down, accepted caveat). Also deleted dead code: calorieColorTier in utils/goalHit.ts (defined, imported nowhere, leftover from the reverted Site 2 home-card color wiring). Both files clean diagnostics.
  [ ] (closed above) GOAL HIT CONSISTENCY original note: app/achievements.tsx around L706 computes its own count with adjustedTarget = nutritionCalTarget + (day.activeCalories ?? 0), then consumed within minus 300 / plus 150. Two problems: (1) it uses RAW activeCalories with NO burn accuracy modifier, and (2) it uses the old calTarget + active double count band instead of the centralized util. achievementData.ts (L1898) and stats.tsx (L404 calendar dots, L572 streak) already route through evaluateCalorieGoalHit in utils/goalHit.ts, so the achievements PAGE can display a different nutrition goal day count than the engine. SPEC_calorie_goal_hit.md audited 6 sites and missed this one (it is effectively site 7). NOW -- Session 64 gym list (Justin, 2026-05-31)

  [~] NULL BMR AUDIT -- verify every net-based calculation in the app gates on bmr > 0. If BMR is 0 (incomplete profile), net calculations silently produce wrong numbers rather than erroring. For Smart Tips: gate any net-based rule on bmr > 0, skip net-based tips entirely if not. App-wide audit needed before TestFlight ships. (NOW -- Session 67)
      AUDIT FINDINGS + FIXES 2026-06-01: root cause traced. computeBmr (utils/calorieTarget.ts) returns 0 when weight is unresolvable; computeDayNet (utils/statsData.ts) has NO guard, so net = consumed - burned (overstated by the full ~1400-1800 kcal BMR) when bmr=0. THREE doors to bmr=0 identified: (1) new user skips the (previously optional) current-weight field in onboarding; (2) Mindful user (weight optional) switches to Balanced/Discipline later; (3) ANY user whose last weigh-in is >30 days old, because resolveWeightForDate capped its lookback at 30 days -> normal-use bug, not just an edge.
      THREE-LAYER FIX (one at a time, all type-clean; NOT yet device-tested):
        [x] Layer 1 -- app/onboarding/your-style.tsx: current weight now REQUIRED to continue for Balanced/Discipline (Continue dims + hint "Enter your current weight to continue"), OPTIONAL for Mindful (Mindful never shows net, confirmed: calorie-card stat row gated styleMode!=='mindful' at index.tsx ~1713, YvY drops 'net' at ~2689). canContinue = selectedMode==='mindful' || parseFloat(currentWeight)>0; guard added to handleContinue too. Closes door 1.
        [x] Layer 2 -- utils/calorieTarget.ts: resolveWeightForDate lookback extended 30 -> 365 days. Used ONLY to feed BMR (confirmed sole caller is loadCalorieTargets:78; NOT the weight-card display), so no display risk. A stale weight gives near-correct BMR; zero gives a wildly wrong net. Closes door 3 for realistic lapses (>1yr caught by layer 3). Existing frozen Day Scores untouched (recompute uses snapshot).
        [x] Layer 3 (ALL display surfaces swept) -- every user-facing net now guards bmr=0: app/(tabs)/index.tsx calorie-card LIVE NET shows "--" + hint "Log your weight to see your calorie net" (non-mindful), YvY 'net' metric todayVal -> null so another metric takes the slot; app/(tabs)/log.tsx Today's Total LIVE NET same dash + hint; app/head-to-head.tsx leaves snap.net null when per-day bmr=0 (metric shows no data); app/day-summary.tsx net line -> null (renders as "--") when frozen dayBmr=0; app/(tabs)/stats.tsx avgNetCals gets its own netDays denominator excluding bmr=0 days, and utils/statsData.ts net graph (ncH) skips plotting bmr=0 days. All net-showing surfaces gated on styleMode!=='mindful' already, so Mindful is untouched. Final backstop, also covers door 2.
      REMAINING (only one, and it's SEPARATE -- belongs to the Smart Tips build, NOT this display audit): the SCORING path. evaluateCalorieGoalHit Way 2 + the Day Score calorie sub use computeDayNet, so a bmr=0 day WITH active burn is scored on a wrong net (generally reads "not hit"). This also flows to calorie achievements / streak / calendar dots / At-a-Glance hit count.   [x] EVR IN-PROGRESS DAY FIX DONE 2026-06-01 (Session 69): generateDiagnosticReport (utils/diagnosticReport.ts) built its 14/30/90 window from offset 0 (today) through windowDays-1, so the current in-progress day was counted in the report. Original gaps (now being closed) below: (1) GOAL SNAPSHOT not stored. computeAndStoreDayScore persists only the DayScore output (composite, label, sub-scores, detail breakdowns, computedAt, version); the goal values (calTarget, paceTarget, proteinGoalG, waterGoal, activeCalGoal, stepGoal, weightGoal) live only on the transient input and are discarded. sleepGoal is the lone exception (already on day.sleepGoal); calorie targets come from the date-keyed loadCalorieTargets(dateKey) which MAY read historical values (verify at build). Need to freeze the goals in effect that day onto the record so forward goal changes never rewrite history. (2) RECOMPUTE-ON-EDIT does not happen. ensureDayScore returns the stored score when a current-version score exists, and the backfill scan skips already-scored days; only a DAYSCORE_VERSION bump or a never-scored day triggers compute. There is no hook on food/water/workout/sleep edits. Confirmed by Justin's forgotten-water example (backfilled 22oz did not move the score). Need an edit-triggered recompute for the affected day, cascading to week + month per 15.5. Independent of Smart Tips code; a Day Score item. (NOW)

  [ ] Advanced Nutrition Card overhaul (log.tsx):
        - Expanded nutrient fields: add more nutrients beyond the current 5.

  [x] AsyncStorage cloud backup AUDIT + journal fix (2026-06-02). The earlier framing ("ALL pj_* keys are local-only") was STALE: cloud sync shipped and works. TWO layers exist: incremental (the storageSet wrapper mirrors each write through syncKey, 131+ call sites) AND a full background sweep (app/_layout.tsx runs uploadAllLocal over every local pj_ key each time the app backgrounds). Did a complete write-by-write audit of every pj_ key in the live code. FINDINGS: the vast majority of real data (daily logs, water, weight, workouts, routines, programs, my_foods, favorites, recipes, exercise_library, profile, settings, streaks, achievements, reading_plans, stats_cards, verse_rotation, tooltips, barcode_overrides) syncs correctly and restores. ONE CRITICAL BUG: the journal (pj_bible_reflections) was excluded from BOTH layers because shouldSync's pj_bible_ exclude prefix (intended only for the re-fetchable pj_bible_{book}_{chapter} cache) also matched it, so journals never reached Firestore and a reinstall or Force Restore would have lost them. FIXED (commit 3b50e9c): added an explicit shouldSync include for pj_bible_reflections so the journal rides both layers. Also routed the remaining raw-written real-ish keys through storageSet for incremental sync (pj_notification_settings, pj_tutorials, the historical goal-snapshot backfill in settings.tsx), though the background sweep already covered them. HARDENED the Force Restore dev tool to run uploadAllLocal BEFORE wiping local, so it can never delete a not-yet-synced key. Correctly-local writes were left alone (tutorial demo entries per the tutorial spec, photo URIs which need the Firebase Storage item, transient handoffs, daily check markers, the restore gate, and the pj_bible_ chapter cache). FOLLOW-UP: existing journal entries upload automatically the next time the app backgrounds with this code (or tap Settings dev tool Upload All Data to do it immediately). Photos remain the separate Firebase Storage migration item. NOW: gym list (2026-06-02)

  [ ] MINDFUL GROWTH AREAS TOGGLE MISSING (found 2026-06-08): mindfulGrowthAreas is a boolean on pj_settings (default false) that controls whether Mindful users receive soft coaching notifications and smart tips. It is already read in smartTipsEngine.ts and utils/dayTakeaway.ts, but there is NO UI to set it anywhere in the app -- not in onboarding, not in settings. Mindful users are permanently locked to growth areas OFF. Fix: add a toggle in Settings under the Coaching Mode section, visible only when styleMode is 'mindful', labeled something like "Allow gentle coaching" or "Show growth areas." One field write to pj_settings. Does not block the notifications build (scheduler reads it correctly, just always false until the toggle exists).

  [ ] SLEEP OVERRIDE / HEALTHKIT CONFLICT: when HealthKit pulls partial or wrong sleep (watch put on mid-night), the user cannot cleanly override it. Manual time entry saves but keeps the HealthKit cycle percentages, so hours and stages mismatch. Fix (whichever is cleaner to build): a conflict prompt when manual times differ significantly from HealthKit times, OR a toggle in the sleep gear / settings modal to override HealthKit entirely for that night. If override is chosen, drop to Path 2 scoring (hours + feel, no stage weighting). Related: smart sleep score and sleep card tips below.
  [ ] MEALTIME DROPDOWN OPENS OFF-SCREEN: on food detail (and possibly recipe log), the add-to-mealtime selector opens downward and renders off-screen near the page bottom, so it looks like nothing happens. Replace with a floating list that pops up above the button, visually detached from page scroll, dismissable by tapping outside. Mini-modal / FAB-expansion feel.
  [ ] FOOD SEARCH FUZZY / SMART MATCHING (investigation first): search is too literal, minor spelling differences stop items surfacing. Spans all search surfaces (recents, my foods, FatSecret results). Exact layer of the problem is TBD; needs investigation before a fix is scoped. Pairs with the recents filter below as a food-search cluster.
  [ ] RECENTS SEARCH FILTER: when the user types a query, their recent foods matching that string should surface at the top of results, above FatSecret results. Same search string, recents just prioritized first.
  [ ] SLEEP CARD TIPS LOW QUALITY (Smart Coach surface): current sleep card tips are barebones and too repetitive. Feed them from the Smart Coach hybrid model when it ships (Family 4 Sleep-Driven), delivered on the sleep card as a NEW surface beyond EvR / Day Summary / Home. Sleep coaching should feel personalized and observational. Surface decision open, discuss alongside faith + notifications surfaces (Question 1). See SMART_COACH_SPEC.md.
  [ ] COMPENSATION PATTERN DETECTION (Smart Coach scenario): significant under-eating the day after a high-calorie day should be flagged as a compensation / restriction pattern. Safety note: a naive engine reads the low day as a big deficit and would PRAISE it, which is exactly the "never celebrate dangerous under-eating" case. Being written into the Smart Coach scenario library this session (Family 3 detection with mandatory Family 9 care framing). See SMART_COACH_SPEC.md.
  [ ] SMART SLEEP SCORE (placeholder, revisit): parked. Justin to revisit when the thought comes back. Lives near the sleep override and sleep card tips items.

  [x] CRITICAL FINDING 2026-06-03, RESOLVED SAME DAY (APP-WIDE, not Faith-only, surfaced while verifying rules for go-live): the live Firestore security rules WERE still Firebase DEFAULT TEST MODE: match /{document=**} { allow read, write: if request.time < timestamp.date(2026, 6, 5); }. TWO problems. (1) SECURITY, live now: any client, even unauthenticated, can read, edit, and delete ALL data in the database (every user's food logs, journals, prayer requests, the works); the top-level ai_usage daily-cap counter is also client-writable, so the cap is currently bypassable. (2) AVAILABILITY, dated: on 2026-06-05 the rule expires and ALL client Firestore access flips to deny, breaking cloud sync and backup app-wide for every user. Must replace with real per-user rules BEFORE June 5 regardless of Faith AI. PLAN (do NOT deploy rules blind): audit every Firestore path the app touches first so new rules break nothing, draft rules locking users/{uid} subtree to its owner and denying client access to top-level ai_usage, verify in the console Rules Playground, then Justin publishes in the console. Real-data integrity is the top priority. RESOLVED 2026-06-03: replaced with real per-user rules (match /users/{userId}/{document=**} allows read+write only if request.auth.uid == userId; ai_usage has NO client rule so it is default-denied; sign-in required, which the app always has before any Firestore call). Audited all client Firestore paths first via the single db instance in firebaseConfig.ts (users/{uid}/days, /store, /prayer_requests) so nothing breaks. Verified in the Rules Playground BEFORE publishing (own-data get = Allow, other-user get = Deny, ai_usage create = Deny), then published in the console; Justin confirmed all data intact after app reload. Rules live console-only (firebase.json has no firestore block, no firestore.rules in repo), so no blind CLI deploy can ever change them. Optional later: version-control the rules as a record, kept disconnected from deploy.
  [ ] RECOMMENDED (Faith AI foundation, flagged 2026-06-03): BUNDLE the full public-domain KJV text into the app. Today data/bible-web.ts holds only the 66-book structure + chapter counts (about 12KB); the verse TEXT is fetched from a third-party GitHub repo (aruljohn/Bible-kjv) and cached in AsyncStorage. Bundling makes Faith AI verse verification truly offline and airtight AND removes a real reliability / supply-chain risk in the EXISTING Bible reader (it breaks offline or if that repo ever goes down or changes). KJV is public domain (roughly 4MB). Its own careful task because it touches the working Bible reader; NOT started. The verse-checker code (Piece 2) is written data-source-agnostic so it already works either way. Also note: data/bible-web.ts is confirmed KJV (the "web" in the name means fetched-from-web, not the WEB translation); a rename is optional cosmetic cleanup.

  BUGS:
  [ ] BUG (ROOT CAUSE CONFIRMED in code 2026-06-03): Workout tab shows YESTERDAY's exercise list after the app sits backgrounded across midnight; only a full app kill fixes it (active-calorie cards were correct, just the exercise list stale). CAUSE: workout.tsx computes `const today = new Date()` and `todayKey` at MODULE LOAD (lines 36-37, module scope), so todayKey freezes to first-bundle-load time and never recomputes. workout.tsx has NO AppState listener and no midnight timer (verified: AppState only exists in _layout.tsx and index.tsx). The cards looked right because they read live HealthKit values, not todayKey, which matches Justin's exact report. NOT a dev-build / Metro / PC-asleep artifact: the phone runs the loaded JS without the PC, and prod apps also resume across midnight, so this survives to TestFlight. FIX: port Home's rollover pattern (index.tsx checkDateRollover ~L926-956: recompute todayKey + day name on AppState 'active' and on a midnight timer). IMPACT CHECK before touching: todayKey is referenced ~12 places in workout.tsx (checks, programs, caloriesBurned writes), so move it into state that updates, do not just patch one read.
  [ ] BUG: Home sleep score did not update this morning until the manual refresh button (app was alive overnight, not killed). LIKELY a HealthKit-not-re-queried-on-resume gap: Home does recompute the date and re-run the day-score scan on AppState 'active' (index.tsx ~L1010), but last night's sleep comes from HealthKit and appears not to be re-pulled on resume, so it reads stale until refresh forces a re-query. Needs a trace of the sleep fetch trigger to confirm (the workout bug above IS confirmed, this one is strong-suspicion). Same family: refresh-on-foreground. NOT a TestFlight-only thing.
  [ ] BUG: Muscle Milk logging mixed oz and mL. Showed 11oz but stored 330 (the mL value); macros + calories were right but Advanced Nutrition was wrong (e.g. potassium read 9600); setting oz to 11 corrected everything. Unit-conversion bug in the logging path. JUSTIN TO SEND SCREENSHOTS of each page + the real Muscle Milk label values before we touch it (needed to deduce exactly where oz/mL crossed).
  [x] BUG: Notifications firing FALSELY. (1) 7pm "Food log reminder, you haven't logged anything today" after logging 3 meals + snacks since 7:40am. (2) 8pm "log gratitude" after gratitude was logged that morning. Fix: cancel-on-action hooks -- food logged cancels pj_food_log, gratitude logged cancels pj_evening_gratitude, water goal crossed cancels pj_water_pace, exercise checked cancels pj_activity. services/notifications.ts (4 cancel exports) + food-detail.tsx + GratitudeStreakCard.tsx + index.tsx + log.tsx + workout.tsx. FIXED 2026-06-08.
  [ ] BUG: EvR hero icons slide off the right edge of the card. Visual clipping.
  [ ] EvR LOGGING-CONSISTENCY DENOMINATOR (2026-06-04 note): the 30-day report shows e.g. "17 of 30 days logged, 57%, looking good," which unfairly punishes a user who has not had the app for a full 30 days. Install and log perfectly for 15 straight days and it reads 15/30 (50%) when the user is really 15/15 (100%). FIX DIRECTION (Justin's lean, confirm before build): denominator = days from the user's FIRST-EVER logged day to today, CAPPED at the report window (30). New users see "X of 15 active days" and only become a true rolling 30 once they pass 30 days of history. Mid-stream skips still count against consistency (that is real inconsistency); only the dead days before they started are excluded. Could label it "X of Y active days" so the number tells the story. Aligns with the weekly-summary philosophy already on the roadmap (excluded/incomplete days do not skew the denominator) and feeds Smart Coach Family 5 (data-quality/confidence). diagnostic-report.tsx.
  [ ] BUG: Macros Today home card gear modal: the dim overlay slides all the way up the screen instead of behaving like a contained modal. Violates the modal/sheet animation standard. index.tsx macros card gear modal.
  [ ] BUG (LOG ONLY, 2026-06-04, not investigating yet): home custom weight LINE GRAPH (graph creator) does not auto-update when a new weight is logged for today. Logging today's weight left the graph unchanged until the duration was toggled 30 to 7 back to 30, which forces a recompute. Classic stale-state: the graph reads its data once and does not re-read on a data change; the duration toggle is what triggers the recompute. Likely fix is a re-read on screen focus or a data-change trigger, but NOT diagnosed in code yet. Same refresh-on-foreground / refresh-on-data-change family as the workout-stale and sleep-score bugs above. Stats graph system.
  [x] RESOLVED 2026-06-03 (verified read-only in code + confirmed live by Justin): "changed yesterday's water, went over goal, but Day Summary score did not change." waterLogged IS in the Day Score data signature (dayScoreStore.ts dataSigFromInput ~L198), so a water edit changes the sig and ensureFreshDayScore recomputes on day-summary open (~L275); Justin confirmed the 13/17 did move on re-check. Related question answered: changing a GOAL in settings does NOT skew past Day Scores; goals are frozen per-day (goalSnapshot) and excluded from the data signature, so history never re-grades on a forward goal change. NUANCE: Day Score / Day Summary are frozen, but EvR (diagnostic report) REGENERATES live each run over completed days, so those two surfaces answer the "will it skew?" question differently by design.

FOUND A REAL BUG, not just drift: the net_carbs_explained tooltip (tooltipRegistry.ts) said net carbs = "total carbs minus fiber" and claimed sugar alcohols were "not yet included, coming in a future update" -- but the actual code subtracts BOTH fiber AND sugar alcohols everywhere (index.tsx:1743, log.tsx:1039, stats.tsx:456: totalCarbs - totalFiber - totalSugarAlcohols). tutorials.ts (281-283) was already correct. FIXED: net_carbs_explained body + Net Carbs def + Sugar Alcohols def now say "minus fiber and sugar alcohols"; worked example updated (Total 35 - Fiber 8 - Sugar Alcohols 2 = Net 25); Settings toggle subtitle (index.tsx:3583) updated to "total minus fiber and sugar alcohols".   [ ] BUG (LOW PRIORITY, edge case): Day Score Recovery can under-credit bedtime consistency on backfilled-only days. sleepConsistencyPts is persisted to the day record ONLY by the home screen when that day is "today" (index.tsx ~1299/2154); day-detail does not re-store it. So a day the user never opened the app on, scored later by the once-a-day backfill scan, reads sleepConsistencyPts ?? 0 and can score its raw sleep up to 10pts low (softened further by the 50pt Recovery floor). Days the user actually used the app on are accurate and match the Sleep card. Verified session 64. Fix options: have the scan compute + persist consistency for the day it scores, or store consistency at sync time independent of the home screen. (SOON)
  [ ] CONSIDER: freeze burn accuracy for STREAKS too (parallel to the Day Score freeze, surfaced 2026-06-01 while scoping Day Score step 3). Confirmed in code: burnAccuracyPct is never stored as data, it is a live multiplier applied as raw activeCalories * pct/100 everywhere. Changing it touches NO stored logged data (food/water/weight/raw watch cals untouched), and does NOT move stored Day Scores (not in the data signature; scores only recompute on data edit / version bump). BUT the auto-tracked streaks in stats.tsx (loadStreaks) recompute live from the daily records each load and apply LIVE burn accuracy: the active-calorie streak and the calorie/net streak will shift retroactively when accuracy changes (e.g. 80 to 100 raises adjusted active cals so more past days clear their goal, lengthening those streaks). The streak GOAL side is already frozen per-day (pj_YYYY-MM-DD.goalSnapshot from the streak-overhaul item), but the burn-accuracy multiplier is not. Step/water/sleep/protein/workout streaks are unaffected (no burn accuracy). Nothing is destroyed (streaks are derived, not stored counts), but counts move. Decision for later: extend the per-day streak goalSnapshot to also freeze burnAccuracyPct so historical streaks lock to the accuracy in effect then, matching the Day Score philosophy. Separate from the Day Score store; lives in stats.tsx loadStreaks. (SOON)

A low target craters Way 1 (no-activity) hit days but not Way 2 (active) days, which judge against the weight-goal pace target, not the calorie number. (SOON)

  Calorie, Goal Logic & Coaching --
  [~] Calorie goal hit logic overhaul -- STATUS: IN PROGRESS (started 2026-05-29). Full build doc: SPEC_calorie_goal_hit.md (decisions locked, do not re-litigate). AUDIT FINDING 2026-05-29: goal-hit is currently computed 6 divergent ways, not 3. Correction to the prior note below: the achievement trigger does NOT do it correctly. It uses RAW active calories (calTarget + data.activeCalories, no burn-accuracy modifier), which is itself a burn-accuracy bug. The 6 sites: (1) achievementData.ts checkNutritionAchievements, (2) home calorie card index.tsx, (3) stats.tsx calendar dots, (4) stats.tsx At a Glance CAL GOAL/DAY count, (5) stats.tsx calorie streak, (6) log.tsx calorie color. This is a rewrite to one shared util (utils/goalHit.ts), not a reconcile.
    LOCKED DECISIONS (2026-05-29, signed off by Justin. See SPEC_calorie_goal_hit.md for worked examples):
    Decision 1: Way 2 hit band is directional +/-150, UNIVERSAL across all modes. Lose: net <= paceTarget+150. Gain: net >= paceTarget-150. Maintain: abs(net) <= 150. The band does not vary by coaching mode (modes change presentation only, because streak/achievement counts are recomputed by re-walking history, so a mode-dependent band would silently rewrite history on toggle).
    Decision 2: Way 1 window keeps the asymmetric -300/+150 against the static calTarget. No net math, no BMR subtraction. The deficit is already baked into calTarget.
    Decision 3: active-cals floor = 50 is the Way 1 vs Way 2 switch. adjustedActive = round((activeCalories||caloriesBurned)*acc/100). Below 50 uses Way 1 (dead/unworn watch guard), 50 or above uses Way 2. Manually logged active cals count, not just HealthKit.
    Decision 4: home/log card color stays graded, but the green/good zone is redefined to mean exactly a hit per Way 1/Way 2, so the card and the streak can never contradict. Non-hit days still split warn vs bad by mode delta. Mindful is neutral, no color.
    DATA CAVEAT (accepted by Justin): moving streak / At-a-Glance count / calendar dots / achievement count onto Way 1/Way 2 will recompute historical numbers up or down. This is a pure display recompute. No pj_ daily record is touched, nothing is deleted or overwritten. Justin's words: "MY streaks changing is whatever, its fine. As long as the logic is good for future stuff and for users starting from scratch."
    BUILD PROGRESS (2026-05-29): utils/goalHit.ts shared util created. Wired: site #1 achievementData.ts (raw-active bug killed), site #4 stats At-a-Glance CAL GOAL/DAY count, site #5 stats calorie streak. Open verification #2 RESOLVED: home card hkCalories already applies burn accuracy (rawHkCalories * burnAccuracyPct / 100), no bug. calorieColorTier made case-insensitive (index uses lowercase styleMode, stats capitalized).
    SITE #2 (home card color) DECISION 2026-05-29: wired then REVERTED to intuitive proximity coloring (consumed vs adjusted target) for the live today-card. Why: today's net uses running BMR, so for a weight-loss goal the net is already a big deficit by midday and the Way 1/Way 2 hit rule flashed the card GREEN before the user finished eating (Justin saw 537/2346 green at lunch). The shared hit logic stays on completed-day surfaces (streak, achievements, At-a-Glance) where full-day net applies and today is excluded from the streak, so nothing contradicts. The "proper" fix is the time-aware deep-deficit color below.
    BUG FIXED 2026-05-29 (pre-existing): stats At-a-Glance CAL GOAL/DAY showed 0/N while the calorie streak showed a real count, because stats read calTarget from pj_settings only (no fallback) and the count was gated behind calTarget>0. Added fallback: pj_settings.calTarget -> pj_profile.calTarget -> computed TDEE+deficit. stats.tsx.
    DECISION 2026-05-29 (At-a-Glance completed-days-only): the period stats now SKIP today (in progress) for calories, macros/net, the cal-goal hit count, water, steps, and active calories. Reason: those accumulate through the day, so a partial today skews the averages and is not a real goal hit yet (matches streak + achievements which already skip today). Today IS still included for workout days, sleep + sleep score (last night is complete), and weight (point-in-time). loadPeriodData in stats.tsx, guarded by isTodayKey. Graphs (fetchTrendData) still plot today as a live point, unchanged.
    NEW IDEA TO BUILD (smart time-aware home card color, approved 2026-05-29): make the today-card color time-of-day aware. Being under target is fine early in the day (green/on-track), but if it is late (e.g. evening) and net is still a deep deficit / consumed is far under, the card should stop reading as a clean green win and signal under-fueling. This is the live-card sibling of the parked "Coaching nudge for very low net days" item and shares its BMR/threshold research (do not guess the hour or the deficit floor). Build together with that nudge once thresholds are confirmed. DEFERRED: site #3 stats calendar day-cell coloring (Justin on the fence, not worth the time/usage right now). The On Target/Close/Off legend pills are HIDDEN as of 2026-05-29 (cell-tint code left in place, restore legend via git if revisited). Side note found while there: the calendar day-cell tint appears invisible in-app even with logged data (suspect calTarget unread at render or sub-0.25-alpha tint washing out on Light theme). Not chased, parked with site #3. Site #6 (log.tsx color) VERIFIED 2026-05-29: log.tsx calorie color is byte-for-byte the same proximity logic as the home card, so it already matches after the home revert. No change needed. Step 6 (head-to-head net) DONE: loadSnapshot repointed at computeDayNet + buildDailyBmrMap. Index YvY net VERIFIED functionally consistent with computeDayNet (minor latent nuance: home YvY ydBmr searches weight from today vs buildDailyBmrMap from that day; negligible, not fixed, low priority). Step 7 (diagnosticReport burn accuracy) DONE: added caloriesBurned fallback at L285. ALL BUILD STEPS COMPLETE except deferred site #3 (calendar coloring). Net result: one shared util (utils/goalHit.ts) drives goal-hit for achievements, the stats calorie streak, and the At-a-Glance count; net flows through computeDayNet everywhere (graph, glance, day-detail, head-to-head); the home + log cards keep intuitive proximity coloring on the live day (Way 1/Way 2 reserved for completed-day surfaces). Burn accuracy confirmed applied or correctly raw at every site.
    POLISH 2026-05-29: Effort vs Results report (diagnostic-report-view.tsx) bold near-black values/headlines switched from theme.textPrimary to theme.textSecondary, matching the softer slate used for the home weight card GOAL / TO GO / PROJECTED values. Status-flagged values still use statusWarn; the Report Not Found error title left as textPrimary.
    Original direction text (still accurate, kept for context):
    Way 2 (primary -- evaluates first): Check true net calories (consumed minus active burn with accuracy modifier applied minus BMR) against the user's daily pace target (e.g. -750 for 1.5 lb/week). If net is within a reasonable range of the pace target, it is a hit. This is the primary check for any user with meaningful HealthKit burn data. What "reasonable range" means needs to be decided during the coding session -- rough idea is +/- 100-150 kcal of the pace target, but this should be tested against real data before locking.
    Way 1 (fallback only): Fires ONLY when active cals are below ~50. This threshold handles: dead watch, no wearable, rest day with zero HealthKit data. Checks consumed vs static calorie target with a tolerance range. Way 1 and Way 2 are mutually exclusive -- Way 2 always takes priority when burn data is present. The ~50 threshold is specifically designed to handle the dead-watch edge case: if a watch dies mid-workout and Apple Health reports 0 active cals, Way 2 would incorrectly evaluate against BMR only and might miss a real hit. The ~50 floor prevents that fallthrough.
    Deep deficit floor (not decided -- research required): If net drops below roughly 40-50% of BMR, still counts as a goal hit but surfaces a coaching nudge (see coaching nudge item below). Does NOT block the achievement or streak. Threshold scales with the user's actual BMR, not a fixed number. Consult dietitian-level guidance before locking this threshold.
    Critical rule: whatever logic is finalized must be byte-for-byte identical in all three places (index.tsx, stats.tsx, achievementData.ts). No paraphrasing, no "close enough." Extract to a shared utility function in utils/ to enforce this. The three-way drift that exists today happened because each location was written separately. It will happen again if the logic is not centralized.
    Related: Way 1 / Way 2 direction explicitly approved as of 2026-05-29 gym session. (CORE COMPLETE 2026-05-29: shared util + all calc sites wired/verified. Only deferred piece is site #3 calendar day-cell coloring, tracked in BUILD PROGRESS above. Close fully when that is built or dropped.)
  [x] Burn accuracy app-wide consistency audit -- DONE 2026-05-29. Every checklist item below confirmed or fixed. No raw HealthKit active-calorie value remains in any user-facing calculation (the only raw reads left are intentional: the burn-accuracy finding showing the device's own number, and relative comparisons where the modifier cancels). Paired with goal hit overhaul, SPEC_calorie_goal_hit.md. The burn accuracy adjustment (100/90/80/70% pill in Settings > Health) must be verified as correctly applied everywhere active calories or net calories appear in a user-facing calculation. The rule is absolute: no raw HealthKit active calorie values in any computation except raw storage writes. Every downstream use must apply the modifier. Storage key confirmed: pj_settings.burnAccuracyPct (default 100).

    - Effort vs Results report in utils/diagnosticReport.ts: FIXED 2026-05-29. The genuine bug was L285 reading d.activeCalories with no caloriesBurned fallback (now d.activeCalories || d.caloriesBurned || 0), so caloriesBurned-only days no longer read as zero active. The other spec-flagged spots were not bugs on inspection: L452/458 compare raw active vs raw average (relative, burn accuracy cancels out), and L617/618 are calTarget*1.1/0.9 against CONSUMED calories (not a burn read at all).   [ ] Weekly pace helper text in settings -- under each pace option in the weight goal / pace picker, show the approximate daily net calorie target needed to stay on pace. These are fixed values from the 3,500 cal/lb rule -- universal science, not personalized to the user:
    Lose 2.0 lb/wk: about -1,000 kcal/day net
    Lose 1.5 lb/wk: about -750 kcal/day net
    Lose 1.0 lb/wk: about -500 kcal/day net
    Lose 0.5 lb/wk: about -250 kcal/day net
    Maintain: about 0 kcal/day net
    (Extend to gain options if the picker supports them)

Must follow the standard pattern: TooltipIcon component, TooltipModal with tooltipKey, new entry in tooltipRegistry.ts.
    This daily pace target should not be a static label only -- it becomes a living reference point that feeds into day summary, weekly summary, and Effort vs Results report. Examples: "You hit -680 net today. Your -750 pace target is close -- a bit more deficit tomorrow puts you back on track." "Avg net this week: -620. Your -750 pace target means you are running about 130 kcal/day light on deficit." Design these integrations in the same session as the settings label, not as separate follow-up work. (SOON)
  [x] NetCalBarChart -- SHIPPED 2026-05-29. Built exactly to this spec; see the full shipped entry in the NOW block above ("NetCalBarChart -- zero baseline SHIPPED 2026-05-29" -- dynamic floating zero baseline, semantic green/amber/red coloring via netSignColor, NetCalLineChart sibling, color picker removed in all three places). This duplicate spec entry is now closed. New dedicated component, spec locked. Replace the current net calories graph with a purpose-built bar chart where the zero baseline is positioned dynamically from the actual data range. Zero line does NOT sit at a fixed vertical midpoint -- it floats to wherever zero falls proportionally within the real min/max spread of the data.
    Behavior spec (locked 2026-05-29 gym session):
    - All deficit days: zero line sits near the top of the chart, all bars point downward, full chart height used. No empty space above the zero line.
    - All surplus days: zero line sits near the bottom, all bars point upward, full chart height used. No empty space below.
    - Mixed days: zero line sits proportionally between data min and max. Surplus bars extend above the line, deficit bars extend below. Proportions reflect the actual ratio between max surplus and max deficit in the dataset.
    - Auto-scales so the tallest bar in either direction always reaches the chart boundary. No wasted whitespace under any data distribution.
    Color: bars below zero (deficit) = muted green (#0d9268). Bars above zero: amber (#d4860a) for modest surplus, red (#cc3333) for large surplus. Threshold between amber and red to be decided during build -- rough idea is surplus above +300 kcal net but test against real data. Zero baseline = textMuted hairline spanning full chart width.
    Interaction: same tap-callout behavior as all other StatsGraphCards. Tap a bar surfaces the date and net value in a callout bubble. Mindful mode: neutral framing on callout -- show the number but no color-coded judgment language in the callout text.
    This is a new component, not a modification to existing bar chart code. Build as a standalone NetCalBarChart in components/ or inline in StatsGraphCard.tsx depending on complexity. (SOON -- spec locked, build when goal hit logic overhaul session is done so the underlying net cal computation is known-correct first)
  [ ] Coaching nudge for very low net days -- when true net (consumed minus active burn with accuracy applied minus BMR) is very low relative to the user's BMR, surface a gentle coaching signal. Exact threshold is NOT decided and must not be guessed -- research direction is below ~40-50% of BMR, but this requires dietitian-level input before a number is locked. Do not build until threshold is confirmed.
    Core rules:
    - Does NOT block the goal hit or the streak. The day still counts as a hit if Way 2 passes.
    - All three coaching styles get the nudge. Delivery is style-specific:
      Discipline: direct, no shame. Example: "Your net was very low today. Make sure you are fueling your effort."
      Balanced: encouraging. Example: "Looks like a big burn day. Try to eat a bit more tomorrow to keep energy up."
      Mindful: no numbers ever in the nudge text. Example: "How are you feeling today? Big active days deserve some extra care." Lower urgency, softer placement -- not a card-level callout.
    - Real harm potential: users logging very low consumed calories alongside high burn should not have that pattern silently validated as a clean win without any signal. Especially relevant for users newer to tracking or with any history around food and body image. The signal is a gentle nudge, not a warning, not blocked. Language bar is high -- must not feel accusatory, clinical, or triggering.
    - Placement not decided: home calorie card subtext, a transient nudge card, day summary section, and morning card are all candidate locations. Needs a design pass before building. Build alongside day summary / morning card / weekly summary features -- those are the natural delivery mechanism.
    - Add a tooltip or help article explaining how calorie goals work, what net calories mean, what burn accuracy does, and a note that very low net days may surface a gentle reminder. Sets user expectations before they encounter the nudge cold.
    - Related to the deep deficit floor note in goal hit logic overhaul item above -- both reference the same BMR threshold.
    - Also drives the SMART TIME-AWARE HOME CARD COLOR (approved 2026-05-29): the live today-card currently uses simple proximity coloring because running-BMR net flashes green mid-day. The time-aware version (under is fine early, deep deficit late in the day is flagged) is the live-card delivery of this same nudge. Build the card color and the nudge together once the hour + deficit-floor thresholds are researched. Do not guess the numbers.
    (SOON -- threshold research required before build, do not build yet)
  [ ] IF integration with low net detection (continue speccing) -- connecting the coaching nudge to IF card state is interesting but complex. Near-term simpler approach that does not require IF integration: use time of day + total consumed by end of day as the signal. If it is late in the day and consumed is very low relative to estimated burn, surface the nudge. This version is straightforward and does not require knowing the user's fasting state.
    Fuller IF-aware version (not ready to build -- needs scoping): app knows the user's eating window from IF start/end times and evaluates intake only within that window. Someone on 16:8 who starts eating at noon should not get flagged at 10am just because they have not eaten -- they are in their fasting window and the flag would be incorrect. This requires: (a) checking IF card state before evaluating the low-net signal, (b) defining what "end of eating window" means for evaluation purposes (window close time vs midnight), (c) handling the user who has not started their fast yet today, (d) handling users who do not use IF at all (falls back to time-of-day signal).
    Open questions before IF-aware spec is locked: what time threshold constitutes "late in the day" for the non-IF fallback, how does the nudge behave if the eating window has not yet closed, does the nudge fire at window-close time or at midnight review. More thought required. Park the IF-aware version and build the simpler time-of-day version first. (SOON -- continue speccing IF-aware version, simpler version buildable after nudge threshold is confirmed)

  tutorialOverrideState pattern -- architectural idea for stateful card tutorials. When a tutorial starts on a card that has multiple UI states driven by real data (IF card: idle/active/eating; sleep card: path 1/2/3; YvY: empty/populated), the card should accept a tutorialOverrideState prop that forces it to render a specific state purely visually -- no AsyncStorage changes, no real data touched. Tutorial engine advances through all states in sequence so every step gets a guaranteed spotlight on the target element. When tutorial ends or is skipped, prop clears and card snaps back to actual state. Primary use case: IF card tutorial so steps 3+4 (TAP WHEN YOU EAT, LAST MEAL) always spotlight correctly regardless of which state the user starts from. Pattern is broadly reusable -- any card with conditional rendering driven by real-time state is a candidate. IFCard is the first implementation target.
  Head-to-Head toolkit -- app/head-to-head.tsx has no (i) tooltip or guided tour. WLT explanation, score bar, delta lines, and the "Results locked at midnight" concept all live here and have no in-app explanation. Needs: tooltipRegistry entry (key: 'head_to_head'), TooltipIcon on the screen header, definitions for Score, Win/Loss/Tie logic (per metric rules), Delta column, Results countdown. This is where WLT explanation belongs -- NOT in the YvY home card tooltip.
  [x] Build-switch data loss fix -- root cause: fire-and-forget syncKey() calls could be lost if iOS suspended the app before Firestore writes completed, meaning today's pj_YYYY-MM-DD data never reached the cloud. Fix: AppState listener in _layout.tsx fires uploadAllLocal() every time the app moves to 'background' state. All 38+ keys pushed to Firestore the moment you background the app. Today's data is in the cloud before you ever touch the build. Fires on 'background' only (not 'inactive') to avoid noisy triggers from notification center/control center. One-way upload, never touches local storage. SHIPPED 2026-05-26.
  Tutorial hidden-card guard -- if a user hides a home card (e.g., IF card removed via Edit Layout) and then launches that card's tutorial from the Home toolkit, the target refs are unregistered and the tutorial runs as a confusing text-only full-screen-dim walkthrough. Correct behavior: check if first step's target key is registered before starting; if not and the tutorial is for a hideable home card, show "The [Card Name] card isn't on your home screen. Add it from Edit Layout to follow along." and cancel. Only home tab card tutorials (cal_card, macros_card, sleep_card, if_card, yvy_card) need this guard -- log/workout/stats/profile screens always have content visible.   [~] SMART TIPS HYBRID PIVOT (2026-06-01): Direction change. Smart Tips is being rebuilt from a pure hardcoded rules engine into a TRUE HYBRID AI COACH. Active source of truth is now SMART_COACH_SPEC.md (SPEC_smart_tips.md + TRIGGER_LIBRARY.md remain the deterministic backbone, not retired).
      ARCHITECTURE: (1) BRAIN = deterministic code. Loads the data window, computes every number, runs scenario detection, decides the headline diagnosis + verdict, assembles a structured packet (named scenario + verdict + supporting facts + mode + faith tier). (2) VOICE = AI at runtime. Receives the packet, writes 2-3 coach sentences in the right coaching mode + faith tier. Never computes a number, never picks the conclusion. (3) CLEANUP = deterministic. Before display/save, verifies every number in the AI output matches a number we sent, strips double dashes, enforces length cap + banned words. Anything off falls back to a safe templated line. AI output is never blindly trusted. Runs once per day per user, cached. Cost a fraction of a cent per tip. Offline / API failure falls back to template.
      WHY: the shipped 40 rules each watch a SINGLE signal and stamp a templated fill-in-the-blank line ("protein below goal 6 of 7 days"). That counts, it does not coach. The multi-signal synthesis layer that connects signals into one conclusion (the North Star) was never built. The fix is multi-signal scenarios carrying real reasoning, voiced by AI. The 40-rule engine becomes the deterministic brain, not throwaway.
      SCENARIO LIBRARY v1 DRAFTED (in SMART_COACH_SPEC.md): 9 families (1 Effort vs Results = foundation, 2 The One Gap, 3 Multi-Signal Patterns, 4 Sleep-Driven, 5 Data Quality/Confidence, 6 Crushing It, 7 Trend/Trajectory, 8 Intermittent Fasting, 9 Safety and Care = overrides all) + a "how the brain chooses" priority spine (Confidence gate > Safety > Effort vs Results > The gap > Positive) + a mandatory accuracy-guards list + the Safety override (never celebrate dangerous under-eating / losing too fast, shift to care, never play doctor, never fear or shame).
      SCENARIO LIBRARY EXPANDED (2026-06-01, Question 1 pass with Justin): added macro gaps (fat/carbs), NEAT collapse, goal-ambition-vs-reality, IF timer + closed-window scenarios, a narrow almost-a-streak nudge, NEW Family 10 Recovery/Readiness + Family 11 Training Patterns, a staleness/flat-line data guard, and [DATA: ready / needs-persistence / needs-build] readiness tags. Decisions: Sleep and Recovery stay SEPARATE families; body recomp + full Momentum/Streaks + Re-engagement + Milestones CUT (overlap achievements/streaks or data-blocked); FAITH integration REOPENED (candidate: a non-EvR surface, was parked secular-only); flagged a TRIGGER_LIBRARY threshold sanity audit. Verified in code: per-workout heart rate + HRV are NOT captured (those scenarios data-gated); resting HR, respiratory rate, blood oxygen, exercise minutes DO store per day. Full detail in SMART_COACH_SPEC.md.
      SHIPPED (2026-06-06): Steps 1-7 all complete. CoachPacket + computeCoachPacket() in smartTipsEngine.ts; coachAI.ts with raw fetch (NOT SDK -- Metro .mjs killed @anthropic-ai/sdk, removed); Home tip card wired (index.tsx); Day Summary Coach Insight card wired (day-summary.tsx); EvR wired (diagnostic-report-view.tsx); privacy.html updated with Anthropic AI disclosure. Family 9 safety gate fixed (requires 3+ weigh-ins AND 5+ calendar day span, not single-day extrapolation). Day Summary ships its own per-day packet (refreshDayCoachTip, pj_coach_tip_day_${dateKey}) using today's data + 7-day context (week avg protein, avg consumed, weight trend) so AI compares today vs the user's own recent pattern. Coach Insight Card visual standard locked: accent-tinted bg, full accent border, centered semibold italic text, hairline separator -- applies to ALL AI coaching surfaces app-wide.
      SHIPPED (2026-06-07): EvR Level 1 packet now fully independent. Three separate cache keys (pj_coach_tip_evr_14/30/90) so each report window stores its own tip. Deduped against home card scenario so EvR never repeats what home already showed. Each window maintains its own scenario rotation via pj_coach_last_rule_evr_${windowDays}. Brain always analyzes most recent 14 days (actionable coaching is current state; expandable to per-window brain data later if 30/90-day-specific scenarios are added).
